}

目前的postionX 和 Y是全局设置的，不同图片由于长宽比不一样，全局设置的位置可能不适合所有图片，有人希望能逐张微调

https://github.com/HowcanoeWang/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/issues/16
> 我日常用笔记本端的思源记笔记，背景一般不开或是模糊，而平板/手机浏览器端用来刷闪卡，这时候开启背景能提高使用意愿，另外，不同宽度设备调整同一张图片xy轴后也会有显示不同

这个需求是否合理？是否会显著增加代码复杂度？应该如何实现？

67: export function render(url: string, forceType?: 'image' | 'video'): void {
68:     const type = forceType ?? detectType(url)
69:     if (type === 'image') renderImage(url)
70:     else if (type === 'video') renderVideo(url)
71: }
72: 
73: export function renderImage(url: string): void {
74:     if (!canvasEl) return
75:     devLog("[bgCover] renderImage:", url.split('/').pop())
76:     currentMode = 'image'
77: 
78:     if (videoEl) {
79:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
80:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
81:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
82:     }
83:     canvasEl.style.display = ''
84:     canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
85:     canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
86: }
87: 
88: export function renderDynamic(url: string, fallbackUrl: string): void {
89:     if (!canvasEl) return
90:     if (videoEl) {
91:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
92:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* ignored */ }
93:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
94:     }
95:     currentMode = 'image'
96:     canvasEl.style.display = ''
97: 
98:     const seq = ++preloadSeq
99:     const preload = new Image()
100:     preload.onload = () => {
101:         if (seq !== preloadSeq || currentMode !== 'image') return
102:         canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`
103:         canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
104:     }
105:     preload.onerror = () => {
106:         if (seq !== preloadSeq) return
107:         canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = `url('${fallbackUrl}')`
108:         canvasEl.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
109:     }
110:     preload.src = url
111: }
112: 
113: export function renderVideo(url: string): void {
114:     if (!videoEl) return
115:     devLog("[bgCover] renderVideo:", url.split('/').pop())
116:     currentMode = 'video'
117: 
118:     if (canvasEl) canvasEl.style.display = 'none'
119:     videoEl.style.display = ''
120:     videoEl.src = url
121:     const playPromise = videoEl.play()
122:     if (playPromise) {
123:         playPromise.catch((e) => {
124:             if (e.name !== 'AbortError') {
125:                 console.warn('[bgCover] video play failed:', e)
126:             }
127:         })
128:     }
129: }
130: 
131: export function clearLayer(): void {
132:     devLog("[bgCover] clearLayer")
133:     if (canvasEl) {
134:         canvasEl.style.display = 'none'
135:         canvasEl.style.backgroundImage = ''
136:     }
137:     if (videoEl) {
138:         videoEl.style.display = 'none'
139:         try { videoEl.pause() } catch { /* not implemented in jsdom */ }
140:         videoEl.removeAttribute('src')
141:     }
142:     currentMode = null
143: }
144: 
145: export function setVisible(visible: boolean): void {
146:     devLog("[bgCover] setVisible:", visible)
147:     if (canvasEl) canvasEl.style.display = visible && currentMode === 'image' ? '' : 'none'
148:     if (videoEl) videoEl.style.display = visible && currentMode === 'video' ? '' : 'none'
149:     if (!visible) {
150:         document.body.style.removeProperty('opacity')
151:     }
152: }
153: 
154: export function changeOpacity(raw: number): void {
155:     const clamped = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(1, raw))
156:     const opacity = 0.99 - 0.25 * clamped
157:     document.body.style.opacity = String(opacity)
158: }
159: 
160: export function changeBlur(val: number): void {
161:     const px = Math.max(0, Math.min(10, val))
162:     const filter = px > 0 ? `blur(${px}px)` : ''
163: 
164:     if (currentMode === 'image' && canvasEl) {
165:         canvasEl.style.filter = filter
166:     } else if (currentMode === 'video' && videoEl) {
167:         videoEl.style.filter = filter
168:     }
169: }
170: 
171: export function changePosition(x: number, y: number): void {
172:     if (currentMode === 'image' && canvasEl) {
173:         canvasEl.style.backgroundPosition = `${x}% ${y}%`
174:     } else if (currentMode === 'video' && videoEl) {
175:         videoEl.style.objectPosition = `${x}% ${y}%`
176:     }
177: }
178: 
179: export function applyOverrides(x?: number, y?: number, defaultX?: number, defaultY?: number): void {
180:     const posX = x ?? defaultX ?? 50
181:     const posY = y ?? defaultY ?? 50
182:     changePosition(posX, posY)
183: }
184: 
185: export function startAutoRefresh(callback: () => void, intervalMs: number): void {
186:     stopAutoRefresh()
187:     if (intervalMs <= 0) return
188:     devLog("[bgCover] startAutoRefresh: interval =", intervalMs, "ms")
189:     autoRefreshTimer = setInterval(callback, intervalMs)
190: }
191: 
192: export function stopAutoRefresh(): void {
193:     if (autoRefreshTimer !== null) {
194:         devLog("[bgCover] stopAutoRefresh")
195:         clearInterval(autoRefreshTimer)
196:         autoRefreshTimer = null
197:     }
198: }

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 18:46:51*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Let me understand the current architecture:

1. **Config (`config.ts`)**: Currently has `positionX` and `positionY` as global settings (default 50, 50)
2. **Type definition**: Let me check the types
3. **`bgRender.ts`**: Has `changePosition(x, y)` and `applyOverrides(x?, y?, defaultX?, defaultY?)` 
4. **There's already `imageOverrides: {}`** in the config! This is likely a mechanism already in place for per-file overrides.

Let me check the types and how `imageOverrides` is currently used.

</details>

131:             createBgLayer()

138:     async randomSelect() {
139:         const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs")
140:         const localFolders = configStore.get("localFolders")
141:         const dynamicBgUrls = configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")
142:         const pool = await scanAll(assetDirs, localFolders, dynamicBgUrls)
143:         if (pool.length === 0) {
144:             devLog("[bgCover] randomSelect: pool is empty, nothing to pick")
145:             return
146:         }
147:         const exclude = pool.length > 1 ? configStore.get("currentFile") : null
148:         const item = pickRandom(pool, exclude)
149:         if (!item) return
150:         devLog("[bgCover] randomSelect: picked", item.name, "from", pool.length, "items")
151:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
152:         configStore.save()
153:         if (item.sourceType === 'dynamic') {
154:             const cb = item.url + (item.url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
155:             renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
156:         } else if (item.type === 'image') {
157:             renderImage(item.url)
158:         } else {
159:             renderVideo(item.url)
160:         }
161:         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
162:         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
163:         changePosition(configStore.get("positionX"), configStore.get("positionY"))
164:     }
165: 
166:     private applyBackground() {
167:         devLog("[bgCover] applyBackground: start")
168:         try {
169:             const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
170:             devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile =", currentFile)
171:             if (!currentFile) {
172:                 devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: currentFile is null, skip render")
173:                 return
174:             }
175: 
176:             if (isDynamicUrl(currentFile)) {
177:                 const cb = currentFile + (currentFile.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
178:                 renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
179:             } else {
180:                 const ext = '.' + (currentFile.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
181:                 devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: ext =", ext)
182:                 if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
183:                     devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderVideo")
184:                     renderVideo(currentFile)
185:                 } else if (IMAGE_EXTS.has(ext)) {
186:                     devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: -> renderImage")
187:                     renderImage(currentFile)
188:                 } else {
189:                     console.warn(`[bgCover] applyBackground: unknown extension "${ext}" for ${currentFile}`)
190:                     return
191:                 }
192:             }
193:         } finally {
194:             const opacity = configStore.get("opacity")
195:             const blur = configStore.get("blur")
196:             const px = configStore.get("positionX")
197:             const py = configStore.get("positionY")
198:             devDebug("[bgCover] applyBackground: changeOpacity =", opacity, "blur =", blur, "pos =", px, py)
199:             changeOpacity(opacity)
200:             changeBlur(blur)
201:             changePosition(px, py)
202:         }
203: 
204:         const interval = configStore.get("autoRefreshTime")
205:         stopAutoRefresh()
206:         if (interval > 0) {
207:             startAutoRefresh(() => this.randomSelect(), interval * 60000)
208:         }
209:     }
210: 
211:     applyThemeShield() {
212:         if (!configStore.get("activate")) return
213:         if (isCurrentThemeDisabled(configStore.get("disabledThemes"))) {
214:             devLog("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme disabled, hiding")
215:             setVisible(false)
216:         } else {
217:             devLog("[bgCover] applyThemeShield: theme enabled, showing")
218:             createBgLayer()
219:             this.applyBackground()
220:         }
221:     }
222: }

<content>
1: import { isDesktop, readLocalDir, getFileUrl, fileExistsLocal } from '../utils/fs'
2: import { readSiyuanDir } from '../utils/api'
3: import type { ImageItem } from '../types'
4: import { pluginAssetsDir, classifyFileType, DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS } from '../constants'
5: import { devDebug } from '../utils/logger'
6: import { toAssetRelPath } from '../utils/path'
7: 
8: const ENGINE = '[bgCover] sourceManager'
9: 
10: export async function scanAll(
11:     assetDirs: string[] = [],
12:     localFolders: string[] = [],
13:     dynamicBgUrls: string[] = [],
14: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
15:     const tasks: Promise<ImageItem[]>[] = [
16:         scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir),
17:         Promise.resolve(scanDynamicUrls(dynamicBgUrls)),
18:     ]
19: 
20:     const validAssetDirs = assetDirs.filter(d => d.length > 0)
21:         .map(dir => {
22:             const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)
23:             return `/data/${normalized}`
24:         })
25:     tasks.push(...validAssetDirs.map(path => scanSource('assets', path + '/')))
26: 
27:     if (isDesktop()) {
28:         const validLocalDirs = localFolders.filter(d => d.length > 0)
29:         for (const dir of validLocalDirs) {
30:             const ok = await validatePath(dir)
31:             if (!ok) {
32:                 devDebug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local[${dir}]: 路径不可访问，跳过`)
33:             } else {
34:                 tasks.push(scanSource('local', dir))
35:             }
36:         }
37:     } else {
38:         devDebug(`${ENGINE} scanAll local: 非桌面端，跳过 ${localFolders.length} 个本地文件夹`)
39:     }
40: 
41:     const batch = await Promise.all(tasks)
42:     const results = batch.flat()
43:     devDebug(`${ENGINE} scanAll total: ${results.length} 个文件`)
44:     return results
45: }
46: 
47: export function scanDynamicUrls(urls: string[]): ImageItem[] {
48:     return urls.map(url => {
49:         const preset = DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.find(p => p.url === url)
50:         return {
51:             name: preset?.name ?? new URL(url).hostname,
52:             url,
53:             apiPath: url,
54:             type: 'image' as const,
55:             sourceType: 'dynamic' as const,
56:             sourceLabel: 'dynamic',
57:         }
58:     })
59: }
60: 
61: export async function scanSource(
62:     type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets',
63:     path: string,
64: ): Promise<ImageItem[]> {
65:     const filenames = type === 'local'
66:         ? await readLocalDir(path)
67:         : await readSiyuanDir(path)
68: 
69:     const items: ImageItem[] = []
70:     const skipped: string[] = []
71: 
72:     for (const name of filenames) {
73:         const fileType = classifyFileType(name)
74: 
75:         if (fileType === null) {
76:             skipped.push(name)
77:             continue
78:         }
79: 
80:         const cleanPath = path.endsWith('/') ? path : path + '/'
81:         const apiPath = `${cleanPath}${name}`
82:         const url = getFileUrl(apiPath, type)
83: 
84:         items.push({
85:             name,
86:             url,
87:             apiPath,
88:             type: fileType,
89:             sourceType: type,
90:             sourceLabel: getSourceLabel(type, path),
91:         })
92:     }
93: 
94:     if (skipped.length > 0) {
95:         devDebug(`${ENGINE} scanSource[${type}] 跳过不可识别的文件: [${skipped.join(', ')}]`)
96:     }
97: 
98:     return items
99: }
100: 
101: export function pickRandom(items: ImageItem[], excludeUrl?: string | null): ImageItem | null {
102:     if (items.length === 0) return null
103: 
104:     if (excludeUrl) {
105:         const filtered = items.filter(item => item.url !== excludeUrl)
106:         if (filtered.length === 0) return null
107:         const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * filtered.length)
108:         return filtered[idx]
109:     }
110: 
111:     const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * items.length)
112:     return items[idx]
113: }
114: 
115: export async function validatePath(path: string): Promise<boolean> {
116:     if (path.length === 0) return false
117: 
118:     if (isDesktop()) {
119:         return fileExistsLocal(path)
120:     }
121: 
122:     try {
123:         await readSiyuanDir(path)
124:         return true
125:     } catch {
126:         return false
127:     }
128: }
129: 
130: function getSourceLabel(type: 'local' | 'upload' | 'assets' | 'dynamic', path: string): string {
131:     switch (type) {
132:         case 'upload':
133:             return 'upload'
134:         case 'assets':
135:             return toAssetRelPath(path)
136:         case 'local':
137:             return path
138:         case 'dynamic':
139:             return 'dynamic'
140:     }
141: }

(End of file - total 141 lines)

<content>
1: <script lang="ts">
2:     import { onMount } from "svelte"
3:     import { configStore } from "../../stores/config"
4:     import { isDesktop } from "../../utils/fs"
5:     import { scanSource } from "../../services/sourceManager"
6:     import { renderImage, renderVideo, renderDynamic, changeOpacity, changeBlur } from "../../services/bgRender"
7:     import { confirmDialog } from "../../libs/dialog"
8:     import { pluginAssetsDir, pickDefaultBackground, DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL, isDynamicUrl } from "../../constants"
9:     import { removeFile } from "../../utils/api"
10:     import { toAssetRelPath } from "../../utils/path"
11:     import { devLog } from "../../utils/logger"
12:     import {
13:         showLocalDirDialog,
14:         showAssetsDirDialog,
15:         showUrlDialog,
16:         showAddDynamicUrlDialog,
17:         setupMultipleFilePicker,
18:         setupFolderFilePicker,
19:     } from "../dialogs"
20:     import type { ImageItem } from "../../types"
21: 
22:     const i18n = (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.i18n ?? {}
23: 
24:     interface SourceGroup {
25:         type: 'upload' | 'assets' | 'local'
26:         label: string
27:         path: string
28:         removable: boolean
29:         files: ImageItem[]
30:         inaccessible: boolean
31:         collapsed: boolean
32:         configKey: string
33:     }
34: 
35:     let groups = $state<SourceGroup[]>([])
36:     let selectedItem = $state<ImageItem | null>(null)
37:     let previewSrc = $state<string | null>(null)
38:     let previewObjectUrl = $state<string | null>(null)
39:     let previewVideoSrc = $state<string | null>(null)
40:     let dynamicCollapsed = $state(false)
41:     let videoNoticeCollapsed = $state(true)
42:     let dynamicUrls = $state<string[]>([])
43:     let customDynamicUrls = $state<string[]>([])
44: 
45:     function presetDisplayName(preset: typeof DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS[number]): string {
46:         return i18n[preset.nameKey] ?? preset.name
47:     }
48: 
49:     onMount(() => {
50:         dynamicUrls = [...configStore.get("dynamicBgUrls")]
51:         customDynamicUrls = [...configStore.get("customDynamicUrls")]
52:         refreshAll()
53:     })
54: 
55:     async function refreshAll() {
56:         const newGroups: SourceGroup[] = []
57: 
58:         const uploadFiles = await scanSource('upload', pluginAssetsDir)
59:         newGroups.push({
60:             type: 'upload',
61:             label: i18n.pluginCache,
62:             path: pluginAssetsDir,
63:             removable: false,
64:             files: uploadFiles,
65:             inaccessible: false,
66:             collapsed: false,
67:             configKey: '',
68:         })
69: 
70:         const assetDirs = configStore.get("assetDirs").filter(Boolean)
71:         const localFolders = isDesktop() ? configStore.get("localFolders").filter(Boolean) : []
72: 
73:         const assetTasks = assetDirs.map(async (dir) => {
74:             const normalized = toAssetRelPath(dir)
75:             const path = `/data/${normalized}`
76:             const label = normalized.startsWith('assets/') ? normalized.slice('assets/'.length) : normalized
77:             const files = await scanSource('assets', path + '/')
78:             return { type: 'assets' as const, label, path, files, normalized }
79:         })
80: 
81:         const localTasks = localFolders.map(async (dir) => {
82:             const files = await scanSource('local', dir + (dir.endsWith('/') ? '' : '/'))
83:             return { type: 'local' as const, label: dir, path: dir, files }
84:         })
85: 
86:         const allScanResults = await Promise.all([...assetTasks, ...localTasks])
87: 
88:         for (const r of allScanResults) {
89:             if (r.type === 'assets') {
90:                 newGroups.push({
91:                     type: 'assets', label: r.label, path: r.path,
92:                     removable: true, files: r.files,
93:                     inaccessible: r.files.length === 0 && r.path.length > 0,
94:                     collapsed: false, configKey: r.normalized,
95:                 })
96:             } else {
97:                 newGroups.push({
98:                     type: 'local', label: r.label, path: r.path,
99:                     removable: true, files: r.files,
100:                     inaccessible: r.files.length === 0,
101:                     collapsed: false, configKey: r.label,
102:                 })
103:             }
104:         }
105: 
106:         groups = newGroups
107:     }
108: 
109:     function togglePreset(url: string) {
110:         if (dynamicUrls.includes(url)) {
111:             dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)
112:         } else {
113:             dynamicUrls = [...dynamicUrls, url]
114:         }
115:         configStore.set("dynamicBgUrls", dynamicUrls)
116:         configStore.save()
117:         if (url === configStore.get("currentFile")) reselectBackground()
118:         refreshAll()
119:     }
120: 
121:     function isPreset(url: string): boolean {
122:         return DYNAMIC_BG_PRESETS.some(p => p.url === url)
123:     }
124: 
125:     function toggleCustomDynamic(url: string) {
126:         if (dynamicUrls.includes(url)) {
127:             dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)
128:         } else {
129:             dynamicUrls = [...dynamicUrls, url]
130:         }
131:         configStore.set("dynamicBgUrls", dynamicUrls)
132:         configStore.save()
133:         if (url === configStore.get("currentFile")) reselectBackground()
134:         refreshAll()
135:     }
136: 
137:     function removeCustomDynamic(url: string) {
138:         dynamicUrls = dynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)
139:         customDynamicUrls = customDynamicUrls.filter(u => u !== url)
140:         configStore.set("dynamicBgUrls", dynamicUrls)
141:         configStore.set("customDynamicUrls", customDynamicUrls)
142:         configStore.save()
143:         if (url === configStore.get("currentFile")) reselectBackground()
144:         refreshAll()
145:     }
146: 
147:     function addDynamicUrl() {
148:         showAddDynamicUrlDialog((url: string) => {
149:             if (!customDynamicUrls.includes(url)) {
150:                 customDynamicUrls = [...customDynamicUrls, url]
151:                 dynamicUrls = [...dynamicUrls, url]
152:                 configStore.set("customDynamicUrls", customDynamicUrls)
153:                 configStore.set("dynamicBgUrls", dynamicUrls)
154:                 configStore.save()
155:                 refreshAll()
156:             }
157:         })
158:     }
159: 
160:     function setDynamicAsBackground(url: string) {
161:         const cb = url + (url.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + '_t=' + Date.now()
162:         configStore.set("currentFile", url)
163:         configStore.save()
164:         renderDynamic(cb, DYNAMIC_BG_FALLBACK_URL)
165:         changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
166:         changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
167:     }
168: 
169:     function toggleGroup(i: number) {
170:         groups[i].collapsed = !groups[i].collapsed
171:         groups = groups
172:     }
173: 
174:     function openAssetDirDialog() {
175:         showAssetsDirDialog((paths: string[]) => {
176:             for (const dir of paths) addAssetFolder(dir)
177:         })
178:     }
179: 
180:     function openLocalDirDialog() {
181:         showLocalDirDialog((path: string) => {
182:             addLocalFolder(path)
183:         })
184:     }
185: 
186:     function addAssetFolder(dir: string) {
187:         if (!dir) return
188:         devLog("[bgCover] addAssetFolder:", dir)
189:         const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs"), dir]
190:         configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
191:         configStore.save()
192:         refreshAll()
193:     }
194: 
195:     function addLocalFolder(path: string) {
196:         if (!path) return
197:         devLog("[bgCover] addLocalFolder:", path)
198:         const folders = [...configStore.get("localFolders"), path]
199:         configStore.set("localFolders", folders)
200:         configStore.save()
201:         refreshAll()
202:     }
203: 
204:     function removeGroup(i: number) {
205:         const g = groups[i]
206:         devLog("[bgCover] removeGroup:", g.type, g.configKey)
207:         const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
208:         const wasCurrentInGroup = g.files.some(f => f.url === currentFile)
209:         if (g.type === 'assets') {
210:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs")]
211:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
212:             if (idx >= 0) {
213:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
214:                 configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
215:                 configStore.save()
216:             }
217:         } else if (g.type === 'local') {
218:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("localFolders")]
219:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
220:             if (idx >= 0) {
221:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
222:                 configStore.set("localFolders", dirs)
223:                 configStore.save()
224:             }
225:         }
226:         clearPreview()
227:         if (wasCurrentInGroup) {
228:             reselectBackground()
229:         }
230:         refreshAll()
231:     }
232: 
233:     function setAsBackground(item: ImageItem) {
234:         devLog("[bgCover] setAsBackground:", item.name)
235:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
236:         configStore.save()
237:         if (item.type === 'image') {
238:             renderImage(item.url)
239:         } else {
240:             renderVideo(item.url)
241:         }
242:     }
243: 
244:     function selectPreview(item: ImageItem) {
245:         if (selectedItem?.url === item.url) {
246:             clearPreview()
247:             return
248:         }
249:         selectedItem = item
250:         if (item.type === 'image') {
251:             loadPreview(item.url)
252:         } else {
253:             previewVideoSrc = item.url
254:         }
255:     }
256: 
257:     function clearPreview() {
258:         if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
259:         selectedItem = null
260:         previewSrc = null
261:         previewObjectUrl = null
262:         previewVideoSrc = null
263:     }
264: 
265:     function loadPreview(url: string) {
266:         if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
267:         previewObjectUrl = null
268:         previewSrc = null
269:         fetch(url)
270:             .then(r => r.blob())
271:             .then(b => {
272:                 if (selectedItem?.url === url) {
273:                     previewObjectUrl = URL.createObjectURL(b)
274:                     previewSrc = previewObjectUrl
275:                 }
276:             })
277:             .catch(() => {})
278:     }
279: 
280:     async function clearCache() {
281:         const group = groups.find(g => g.type === 'upload')
282:         if (!group || group.files.length === 0) return
283:         const imgCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'image').length
284:         const vidCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'video').length
285:         const parts: string[] = []
286:         if (imgCount > 0) parts.push(`${imgCount} ${i18n.imageCount}`)
287:         if (vidCount > 0) parts.push(`${vidCount} ${i18n.videoCount}`)
288:         const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>(resolve => {
289:             confirmDialog({
290:                 title: i18n.clearCacheTitle,
291:                 content: `${i18n.clearCacheConfirm} ${parts.join('、')}`,                confirm: () => resolve(true),
292:                 cancel: () => resolve(false),
293:                 width: "360px",
294:             })
295:         })
296:         if (!confirmed) return
297:         devLog("[bgCover] clearCache:", group.files.length, "files")
298:         const wasCurrentDeleted = group.files.some(f => f.url === configStore.get("currentFile"))
299:         for (const file of group.files) {
300:             await removeFile(file.apiPath)
301:         }
302:         if (wasCurrentDeleted) await reselectBackground()
303:         refreshAll()
304:     }
305: 
306:     function openInFileManager(group: SourceGroup) {
307:         const wsDir = (window as any).siyuan?.config?.system?.workspaceDir ?? ''
308:         let absPath = group.path
309:         if (group.type === 'upload' || group.type === 'assets') {
310:             absPath = wsDir + absPath
311:         }
312:         try {
313:             const shell = (window as any).require?.('electron')?.shell
314:             if (shell) {
315:                 shell.openPath(absPath)
316:             } else {
317:                 const { exec } = (window as any).require?.('child_process') ?? {}
318:                 if (exec) {
319:                     const cmd = process.platform === 'darwin' ? 'open' : process.platform === 'win32' ? 'explorer' : 'xdg-open'
320:                     exec(`${cmd} "${absPath}"`)
321:                 }
322:             }
323:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
324:     }
325: 
326:     async function reselectBackground() {
327:         configStore.set("currentFile", null)
328:         await configStore.save()
329:         await (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.randomSelect?.()
330:         if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
331:             configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
332:             await configStore.save()
333:             ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyBackground?.()
334:         }
335:     }
336: 
337:     async function deleteFile(file: ImageItem) {
338:         devLog("[bgCover] deleteFile:", file.name)
339:         const wasCurrent = file.url === configStore.get("currentFile")
340:         await removeFile(file.apiPath)
341:         if (wasCurrent) await reselectBackground()
342:         refreshAll()
343:     }
344: 
345:     function pickMultipleFiles() {
346:         setupMultipleFilePicker(() => { refreshAll() })
347:     }
348: 
349:     function pickFolderFiles() {
350:         setupFolderFilePicker(() => { refreshAll() })
351:     }
352: 
353:     function showAddUrlDialog() {
354:         showUrlDialog((uploadUrl?: string) => {
355:             if (uploadUrl) {
356:                 configStore.set("currentFile", uploadUrl)
357:                 configStore.save()
358:                 if (uploadUrl.match(/\.(mp4|webm|ogg|mov|avi|mkv)$/i)) {
359:                     renderVideo(uploadUrl)
360:                 } else {
361:                     renderImage(uploadUrl)
362:                 }
363:                 changeOpacity(configStore.get("opacity"))
364:                 changeBlur(configStore.get("blur"))
365:             }
366:             refreshAll()
367:         })
368:     }

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 18:46:51*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Now I have a thorough understanding of the codebase. Let me analyze the feature request:

## Current State

1. **`ImageOverride` type already exists** in `types.ts` with `positionX?` and `positionY?` fields
2. **`imageOverrides: Record<string, ImageOverride>`** already exists in `AppConfig` config with default `{}`
3. **`applyOverrides(x?, y?, defaultX?, defaultY?)`** function already exists in `bgRender.ts` but is **never called anywhere**
4. Currently `positionX`/`positionY` are global settings, used everywhere in `index.ts` (lines 163, 201), `ConfigTab.svelte` (lines 37, 66, 75)

So the infrastructure for per-file overrides is basically already built but not wired up!

## Analysis

### Is the feature request reasonable?
Yes, very reasonable. Different images have different aspect ratios (landscape vs portrait, panoramas, etc.), and `cover` cropping with a single global position won't look good for all of them. The user in the issue also mentions different device widths.

### Will it significantly increase code complexity?
No, because the data structure already exists! `ImageOverride` and `imageOverrides` are already defined. The main work is:

1. Wire up `applyOverrides` in `index.ts` to check `imageOverrides` for the current file
2. Add per-file position UI in preview/SourcesTab or a new UI element
3. Add a per-file config key in `i18n` translations

Let me think about the design more carefully.

### Design Decisions

**What should be the "key" in `imageOverrides`?**

Currently `currentFile` stores the full URL/API path of the file. For `imageOverrides` mapping:
- For `upload` files: `public/{packageName}/file.jpg` 
- For `assets` files: `assets/.../file.jpg`
- For `local` files: `file:///home/user/Pictures/file.jpg`
- For `dynamic` URLs: the full URL

The `currentFile` is already used to identify the current background - but the issue is that these URLs can be quite long. However since the type is already `Record<string, ImageOverride>`, using the same `currentFile` value as key makes sense.

Wait, looking more carefully: the `currentFile` can change (when random select picks a new file), and the key would be the full URL. Let me check what values `currentFile` takes...

From the config:
```json
"currentFile": "assets/title/subfolder2/GqqxP-AWkAAys85.jpg"
```

And in `randomSelect()`:
```ts
configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
```

And in `setAsBackground()`:
```ts
configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
```

The `item.url` comes from `getFileUrl(apiPath, type)` which returns:
- local: `file:///absolute/path`
- upload: something like `public/{packageName}/img.jpg` (relative webview path)
- assets: `assets/.../img.jpg` (relative webview path)

So the key would be the URL form. That's workable but a bit fragile if paths change. However for an MVP this is fine.

**Where to put the per-file position UI?**

The most natural place is in the `SourcesTab` preview area. When a user hovers over a file and the preview shows, they could have sliders there to adjust position for that specific file. Currently the preview area at line 622-634 just shows the image/video. We could add position sliders there.

Alternatively, since the feature is about fine-tuning, maybe we need a config per file accessible from the file list entry. But that would clutter the list.

The simplest and most intuitive approach: When a user has selected a file as preview, show position sliders in the preview panel that save to `imageOverrides` for that file's URL. Also, when the current background is set, use `applyOverrides` to check for per-file overrides.

**Should this affect the global position settings?**

I think the design should be:
1. Global `positionX`/`positionY` remain as defaults
2. Per-file overrides in `imageOverrides[currentFile]` take priority when rendering
3. The ConfigTab sliders continue to work as global defaults
4. In SourceTab preview, when a file is selected, sliders adjust per-file overrides

Let me now check the i18n files to see what keys exist.

</details>

Now I have a complete picture. Let me summarize my analysis and present the plan to the user.

## Key Findings

1. **The infrastructure already partially exists but is not wired up:**
   - `ImageOverride` type with `positionX?` and `positionY?` already defined
   - `imageOverrides: Record<string, ImageOverride>` already in config with `{}` default
   - `applyOverrides(x?, y?, defaultX?, defaultY?)` function already in `bgRender.ts` but **never called**

2. **What's missing:**
   - Wire up `applyOverrides` in `index.ts` (both `applyBackground()` and `randomSelect()`) to check `imageOverrides[currentFile]`
   - UI for editing per-file overrides (in SourcesTab preview area)
   - Actually using the existing `applyOverrides` function

## Complexity Analysis

The change is minimal:
- `index.ts`: ~5 lines changed (use `applyOverrides` with per-file values)
- `SourcesTab.svelte`: add position sliders in preview panel (~30 lines)
- `ConfigTab.svelte`: no change needed (global settings stay)
- `i18n`: 2-3 new keys for the UI labels
- `bgRender.ts`: `applyOverrides` already exists, no change needed

## Key Design Decision: What key to use for `imageOverrides`?

The `currentFile` stores values like:
- `assets/title/subfolder2/GqqxP-AWkAAys85.jpg`
- `public/siyuan-plugin-background-cover/img.jpg`
- `file:///home/user/Pictures/img.jpg`

Using the same URL format as `currentFile` as the key is the natural choice since we're looking up per-file overrides when rendering the current background.

## Concerns:
1. **Path stability**: If a user renames a file or moves it, the override is orphaned. But this is minor and could be cleaned up later.
2. **Dynamic URLs**: For dynamic URLs (which return different images each time), per-file position overrides don't make sense. They should be skipped.
3. **Where to put the per-file UI**: The preview panel in SourcesTab is the most natural place. When a user selects a file, they can adjust position. This also gives real-time visual feedback.

Let me present this analysis clearly.

</details>

## 分析

### 需求合理性：**合理**

不同图片长宽比差异大（横版 vs 竖版、全景图等），全局 `cover` 裁剪位置不可能适配所有图片。issue 提到的多设备场景也成立。

### 代码复杂度：**几乎不增加**

好消息：基础架构已经存在但未接线。

- `ImageOverride { positionX?, positionY? }` 类型已定义（`src/types.ts:6-9`）
- `imageOverrides: Record<string, ImageOverride>` 已在配置中（`src/types.ts:24`）
- `applyOverrides(x?, y?, defaultX?, defaultY?)` 函数已实现（`src/services/bgRender.ts:179-183`）但**从未被调用**

### 实现计划

需要改动的文件和内容极少：

| 文件 | 改动 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| `src/index.ts` | ~5行 | `applyBackground()` 和 `randomSelect()` 中，根据 `currentFile` 查 `imageOverrides` 并调用 `applyOverrides`，fallback 到全局 `positionX/Y` |
| `src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte` | ~30行 | 预览面板加 per-file 位置滑块，改动写入 `imageOverrides` |
| `public/i18n/*.json` | 2个新 key | `perFilePosition` / `resetPerFilePosition` |

**不改动的文件**：
- `ConfigTab.svelte` — 全局位置滑块保持原样
- `bgRender.ts` — `applyOverrides` 已存在，无需改动
- `types.ts` / `config.ts` — 类型和默认值已有

**关键设计点**：
- `imageOverrides` 的 key 用 `currentFile` 相同的 URL 格式（与 `setAsBackground` 一致）
- 动态 URL 源跳过 per-file override（每次返回不同图片，设置无意义）
- 预览面板新增滑块，实时生效，改动写入 `imageOverrides`，同时设置一个"重置"按钮将该文件 override 删除

Let me think about the design carefully.

### Key Design Decisions:

- Remove `positionX`, `positionY` from `AppConfig` type
- Remove the slider UI from ConfigTab

- When user adjusts X/Y sliders for current background, write to `imageOverrides[currentFile]`
- If slider is set to 50/50, remove the override (clean up)
- In render path, check `imageOverrides[currentFile]`, fallback to `{positionX: 50, positionY: 50}`

**4. File list markers**
- In the file items within groups, after the filename, show `(x:50%, y:45%)` if override exists

**5. Resolution-based axis disabling**
- When loading an image, we can get its natural dimensions
- In `cover` mode, if the image aspect ratio is wider than the viewport, Y is irrelevant (top/bottom are cropped). If taller, X is irrelevant.
- This requires knowing the image dimensions and the viewport aspect ratio
- This is a nice-to-have, complex to implement reliably. Let me think about how to do this...

For `background-size: cover`:
- The image is scaled to cover the entire container while preserving aspect ratio
- If image AR > container AR → image is wider, left/right get cropped, so Y slider is irrelevant
- If image AR < container AR → image is taller, top/bottom get cropped, so X slider is irrelevant
- If equal, both are irrelevant (but unlikely)

To implement this, we'd need:
- Get image natural dimensions (from an Image() preload or from the preview)
- Get viewport dimensions
- Compare aspect ratios
- Disable the irrelevant slider

This adds significant complexity. The image could be loaded at different times, viewport can change (resize, mobile/desktop). Let me suggest making this an optional enhancement.

Actually, wait - let me think about this more carefully. The user says "x和y本质上只能调整一个". That's not exactly true for `background-position` with `cover`. Let me think...

With `background-size: cover` and `background-position: X% Y%`:
- If the image is wider than the container (AR > container AR), the image height matches container height exactly, and excess width is cropped. Moving X% changes which part of the width is visible. Moving Y% does nothing because the height is exactly matched.
- If the image is taller than the container (AR < container AR), the image width matches container width exactly, and excess height is cropped. Moving Y% changes which part of the height is visible. Moving X% does nothing.

So yes, exactly one axis matters. Good observation.

To implement this, we need:
1. When setting the current background, load the image to get natural dimensions
2. Compare with viewport dimensions
3. Disable the irrelevant slider

But this has edge cases:
- Videos don't have natural dimensions the same way
- Canvas viewport can be different from window viewport
- Dynamic URLs don't have a fixed dimension

I think we should treat this as a nice-to-have for a follow-up. The core feature (per-file position) is already valuable without it.

**6. Migration path**
- On first load after update, if `positionX` and `positionY` exist in config and don't equal defaults (50, 50), migrate them to `imageOverrides[currentFile]`
- Then remove `positionX` and `positionY` from the config schema

> 去掉全局位置这个概念，新文件默认 50/50

### Plan

#### Phase 1: Data layer changes

**`src/types.ts`:**
- Remove `positionX`, `positionY` from `AppConfig`
- Keep `imageOverrides: Record<string, ImageOverride>`

**`src/stores/config.ts`:**

- Add migration: on load, if old `positionX`/`positionY` exist, migrate to `imageOverrides[currentFile]`

#### Phase 2: Service layer changes

**`src/services/bgRender.ts`:**
- `applyOverrides()` already exists, but it takes x,y,defaultX,defaultY individually. We should change it to accept `ImageOverride | null` and a defaults object, or just simplify to always use it.

Actually, let me look at `applyOverrides` again:

```ts
export function applyOverrides(x?: number, y?: number, defaultX?: number, defaultY?: number): void {
    const posX = x ?? defaultX ?? 50
    const posY = y ?? defaultY ?? 50
    changePosition(posX, posY)
}
```

This is already fine. In `index.ts`, we'd call:
```ts
const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[currentFile]
applyOverrides(override?.positionX, override?.positionY, 50, 50)
```

**`src/index.ts`:**
- In `applyBackground()` and `randomSelect()`: replace `changePosition(px, py)` with override-aware call
- Remove reading `positionX`/`positionY` from config

#### Phase 3: UI changes

**`src/ui/settings/ConfigTab.svelte`:**
- Remove the "当前背景" section (lines 53-79) - the `<label>` with currentFile and X/Y sliders
- Remove `positionX`/`positionY` state variables
- Keep: activate toggle, auto refresh, opacity, blur

**`src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte`:**
- Add "当前背景" display at top with per-file X/Y sliders
- Add override markers in file list items
- Load image dimensions for axis disabling (optional)

#### Phase 4: i18n changes

- Add keys for "单独位置" or "perFilePositionHint", "resetPosition", "positionOverride"

#### Phase 5: Image dimension detection (optional)

This is complex. Let me think about the implementation:

1. When user selects a file as background, preload the image
2. Get `img.naturalWidth` and `img.naturalHeight`  
3. Compare with viewport to determine which axis matters
4. Store in override or derive on-the-fly

Actually, we don't need to store the dimensions. We can derive which axis is relevant each time:
- If `imgAR > viewportAR`, disable Y slider
- If `imgAR < viewportAR`, disable X slider

But the SourcesTab preview loads via fetch→blob→createObjectURL, not directly as an Image(). We'd need to create an Image element to get natural dimensions.

Also, for the "current background" position sliders in SourcesTab, the image is already being displayed. We can look at the canvas element's computed style or create a temporary Image().

This is doable but adds about 20-30 lines of code. Let me include it in the plan but mark as optional.

Actually, thinking more about how cover works:

For `background-size: cover` on a container of size `W×H`:
- Scale factor = max(W/imgW, H/imgH)
- Displayed size = imgW * scale × imgH * scale
- If imgW * scale > W, horizontal cropping occurs (X matters, Y doesn't)
- If imgH * scale > H, vertical cropping occurs (Y matters, X doesn't)
- If both equal, no cropping (both don't matter, image fits exactly)

The condition `imgW * scale > W` is equivalent to `imgW / imgH > W / H` (i.e., image is wider aspect ratio than container).

So the logic is simply:
```ts
const imgAR = naturalWidth / naturalHeight
const containerAR = containerWidth / containerHeight
const xRelevant = imgAR > containerAR  // wider image: horizontal crop
const yRelevant = imgAR < containerAR  // taller image: vertical crop
// if equal, both are relevant (but practically never happens)
```

For the sliders in SourcesTab, the container is the preview panel which has a fixed aspect ratio? No, it's flex-based. But we can use `window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight` as the viewport ratio.

Let me simplify: we can use `document.documentElement.clientWidth / document.documentElement.clientHeight`.

For now, let me include the resolution detection in the plan but mark it as optional/follow-up since it's a separate concern.

### Migration concerns

The `positionX`/`positionY` removal from AppConfig breaks backward compatibility. The config is stored in localStorage/siyuan storage. When the plugin loads:
1. Old config has `positionX: 55, positionY: 55`  
2. New code reads it, maps to `AppConfig` which no longer has these fields
3. The spread `{ ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }` will include the old values in `this.cfg` object
4. But `this.cfg` is typed as `AppConfig` which no longer has `positionX`/`positionY`

The safe approach: keep positionX/Y in the type for backward compat during migration, or do a one-time migration in the `load()` method.

Actually, since `this.cfg` is typed and uses `{ ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }`, the old keys will still be in the object (spread preserves all keys), they just won't be accessible by type. When we call `save()`, `setLocalStorageVal` will write the full object including old keys.

Better approach for migration:
```ts
async load() {
    // ...existing code to get stored...
    this.cfg = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }
    
    // Migration: move old global position to per-file override
    if (stored?.positionX !== undefined || stored?.positionY !== undefined) {
        const currentFile = this.cfg.currentFile
        if (currentFile) {
            this.cfg.imageOverrides[currentFile] = {
                positionX: stored.positionX ?? 50,
                positionY: stored.positionY ?? 50,
            }
        }
        // Remove old keys from stored object by not persisting
        this.dirty = true
    }
}
```

Actually, the stored object might still contain the old keys. We should clean them on save or just accept that they'll linger. The simplest approach: keep `positionX`/`positionY` in the type but mark as deprecated and never read them. OR remove them and handle the migration.

Let me think about the cleanest approach:

1. Remove `positionX`/`positionY` from `AppConfig` type
2. In `load()`, after merging, migrate old values to `imageOverrides[currentFile]`, then delete the old keys from `this.cfg`
3. On next `save()`, the old keys are gone

But we can't delete typed properties easily in TS. Let me use a different approach:

```ts
async load() {
    // ...
    const raw = { ...APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS, ...stored }
    
    // Migration: move old global position to per-file override
    const oldX = (stored as any)?.positionX
    const oldY = (stored as any)?.positionY
    if ((oldX !== undefined && oldX !== 50) || (oldY !== undefined && oldY !== 50)) {
        if (raw.currentFile && !raw.imageOverrides[raw.currentFile]) {
            raw.imageOverrides[raw.currentFile] = {
                positionX: oldX ?? 50,
                positionY: oldY ?? 50,
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Strip old keys
    delete (raw as any).positionX
    delete (raw as any).positionY
    
    this.cfg = raw as AppConfig
    this.dirty = true // force save to clean old keys
}
```

This is clean. Let me finalize the plan.

3. Pre-compute and store `relevantAxis: 'x' | 'y' | 'both'` in `ImageOverride`

Option 2 (on-the-fly) is simplest but requires loading the image. Option 1 requires storing dimensions which can be large numbers. Option 3 pre-computes but needs to be stored.

Actually, a simpler approach: when setting per-file position, create a temporary `Image()` to get dimensions, then derive which axis is relevant from the current viewport ratio. This is cheap (image is cached by browser).

Let me propose: include the dimension detection as part of the plan, but keep it simple:
- When adjusting position for an image, load it to get dimensions
- Compare with viewport AR
- Disable irrelevant slider with a tooltip explaining why
- Skip for videos and dynamic URLs

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

The user wants me to finalize the plan, including Phase 5 (resolution detection for disabling irrelevant axis). Let me think through the Phase 5 design in detail.

For `background-size: cover`:
- The image is scaled to cover the entire container while preserving aspect ratio
- The scaling factor is `max(containerW / imgW, containerH / imgH)`
- After scaling, the displayed image size is `imgW * scale × imgH * scale`
- If `imgW * scale > containerW`: horizontal overflow → X slider is relevant, Y is not
- If `imgH * scale > containerH`: vertical overflow → Y slider is relevant, X is not
- These two conditions are equivalent to comparing aspect ratios:
  - `imgAR > containerAR` → image is wider → X matters, Y doesn't
  - `imgAR < containerAR` → image is taller → Y matters, X doesn't
  - `imgAR === containerAR` → perfect fit → both don't matter

Where to get container dimensions? For the background canvas, it spans the entire viewport (100% width, 100% height), so we use `document.documentElement.clientWidth / clientHeight`.

But there's a subtlety: the canvas element is positioned at `width: 100%; height: 100%` on the document element. The actual rendered area is the viewport. So `document.documentElement.clientWidth / clientHeight` is correct.

For the SourcesTab preview panel, the container is the preview div, but the background position is about the full-page rendering, so we should always use viewport dimensions.

Now, where to load image dimensions:

1. **In `setAsBackground()` in SourcesTab**: When user clicks to set background, we can preload the image to get dimensions.
2. **In `applyBackground()` in index.ts**: When applying background on startup.
3. **In `randomSelect()` in index.ts**: When random selecting.

The dimensions need to be stored somewhere so that the SourcesTab sliders can know which axis to disable. Options:

a. Store `naturalWidth`/`naturalHeight` in `ImageOverride` → bloats config
b. Store a computed `relevantAxis: 'x' | 'y' | 'both'` in `ImageOverride` → compact but needs recomputation on viewport change
c. Compute on-the-fly when showing the sliders → needs image loading, may be slow
d. Store both width/height and compute relevant axis on-the-fly from current viewport → best of both worlds

Actually, let me reconsider. The viewport AR can change (window resize, different devices). So storing a pre-computed `relevantAxis` is wrong — it depends on current viewport.

The cleanest approach:
- Store `naturalWidth` and `naturalHeight` in `ImageOverride` (optional fields)
- When showing the sliders, compute relevant axis from stored dimensions + current viewport AR
- This handles viewport changes correctly

But wait, storing width/height for every file in `imageOverrides` bloats the config. And for videos, we need different handling.

Alternative: Don't store anything. When showing the current background sliders, load the image to get dimensions. The image is already cached by the browser (it's the current background), so this is essentially free. For the initial load, we can preload it.

Let me think about the flow:

1. User clicks "设为背景" on a file → `setAsBackground(item)` is called
2. We render the image, then load it in a background Image() to get dimensions
3. Store dimensions in `imageOverrides[url]` only if user adjusts position (so we can compute relevant axis later)

Actually, the simplest approach for Phase 5:

**In SourcesTab, when showing the "当前背景" position sliders:**
- If `currentFile` is an image (not video, not dynamic), create `new Image()`, set src, read `naturalWidth`/`naturalHeight`
- Compare AR with viewport AR
- Disable irrelevant slider
- Cache dimensions in a local variable to avoid re-loading on every render

**In setAsBackground():**
- After setting background, also trigger dimension detection

Let me think about the implementation in SourcesTab context:

```svelte
<script>
let imageDims = $state<{ w: number; h: number } | null>(null)
let containerAR = $state(1)
let xDisabled = $state(false)
let yDisabled = $state(false)

function updateImageDims() {
    const cf = configStore.get("currentFile")
    if (!cf || isVideo(cf) || isDynamicUrl(cf)) {
        imageDims = null
        return
    }
    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => {
        imageDims = { w: img.naturalWidth, h: img.naturalHeight }
        updateDisabledAxes()
    }
    img.src = cf
}

function updateContainerAR() {
    containerAR = document.documentElement.clientWidth / document.documentElement.clientHeight
    updateDisabledAxes()
}

function updateDisabledAxes() {
    if (!imageDims) {
        xDisabled = false
        yDisabled = false
        return
    }
    const imgAR = imageDims.w / imageDims.h
    xDisabled = imgAR < containerAR - 0.01  // image taller, X doesn't matter
    yDisabled = imgAR > containerAR + 0.01  // image wider, Y doesn't matter
}
</script>
```

This is clean. Let me finalize the design.

For videos (object-fit: cover): same logic applies, but we can get `videoWidth`/`videoHeight` from the video element. However, for simplicity, I'll skip video dimension detection in Phase 5.

For dynamic URLs: skip entirely.

**Storage of dimensions in imageOverrides:**

I think we should NOT store dimensions in the config file. Instead, compute on-the-fly:
- When SourcesTab mounts or currentFile changes, load image to get dims
- When viewport resizes, recompute
- The image is already cached (it's the current background), so load is instant

This avoids config bloat and handles viewport changes.

Let me also think about the slider interaction more carefully.

When user adjusts X slider for the current background in SourcesTab:
1. `oninput`: call `changePosition(x, y)` on canvas/video for real-time preview
2. `onchange`: write to `imageOverrides[currentFile]` and save config

If user sets both to 50/50 (default), we should remove the override entry to keep config clean.

For the file list marker `(x:55%, y:40%)`: check `imageOverrides[file.url]` for each file item.

OK, let me now formalize the complete detailed plan.

Wait, one more thing: the user said the old positionX/Y in ConfigTab should move to SourcesTab as per-file adjustments. But there's also the SourcesTab preview panel. Currently:
- Preview panel is for hovering over files (mouseover preview)
- The "当前背景" block at top is for the currently active background

These are different. The per-file position sliders should be for the CURRENT background (top block), not for the previewed file. But the user might also want to adjust position for a file they're previewing (not necessarily the current background).

Hmm, let me re-read the user's request:
> 移动到 数据管理 sourcesTab内的顶部
> 当前背景 url x y 滑块 → 用于调整当前的背景

So only adjust the CURRENT background position from SourcesTab. Not per-preview-file. That makes sense — the preview is just a preview, and adjusting its position would be confusing since it's not the live background.

But we need to support per-file overrides. The flow would be:
1. User sets file X as background (clicks "设为背景")
2. User adjusts position sliders for X → saved to `imageOverrides[X.url]`
3. User later sets file Y as background
4. Y starts with default 50/50. If Y had a previous override, it's applied.
5. User re-selects X → X's override is applied automatically

This naturally works because we always check `imageOverrides[currentFile]` when rendering.

Now, the file list markers help: if user sees `(x:55%, y:40%)` next to a file, they know that file has a custom position.

One more thing: the migration. The user's current config has `positionX: 55, positionY: 55`. We should migrate this to `imageOverrides[currentFile]` on first load.

Final edge case: when user opens SourcesTab, the "当前背景" sliders should reflect the current file's override (or 50/50 if none). This means reading from `imageOverrides[currentFile]`.

Let me now write the complete plan.

---

## Phase 5 详细设计：分辨率检测 + 无效轴禁用

### 原理

`background-size: cover` 下，图片 AR 与视口 AR 比较决定哪个轴有效：

| 条件 | 说明 | 结果 |
|------|------|------|
| `imgAR > viewportAR` | 图比屏幕宽 | Y 禁用（高度刚好填满） |
| `imgAR < viewportAR` | 图比屏幕高 | X 禁用（宽度刚好填满） |
| `imgAR ≈ viewportAR` | 几乎匹配 | 两者均可 |

> 容差设为 ±0.01 避免浮点误差

### 实现方式：**运行时计算，不存配置**

```
SourcesTab mount / currentFile 变化
    │
    ├─ 是视频？ → 跳过，两轴皆可用
    ├─ 是动态 URL？ → 跳过，两轴皆可用
    └─ 是图片 URL：
          │
          new Image().src = url   ← 浏览器已缓存，几乎零延迟
          │
          img.onload:
            imgAR = naturalWidth / naturalHeight
            viewportAR = document.documentElement.clientWidth
                       / document.documentElement.clientHeight
            │
            ├─ imgAR > viewportAR + 0.01  → yDisabled = true
            ├─ imgAR < viewportAR - 0.01  → xDisabled = true
            └─ else                       → 两者皆可用
```

**不存入 `imageOverrides`** 的理由：
1. 避免配置膨胀
2. 视口会变（窗口 resize、不同设备），存预计算值不准确
3. 图片已缓存，`new Image()` 加载即时完成

### 被禁用的滑块表现

```html
<input class="b3-slider" type="range" disabled
       title="图片高度刚好填满，此方向无法调整" />
```

- `disabled` 属性置灰
- tooltip 解释原因（via `b3-tooltips` 或原生 `title`）
- 绑定的 `positionX`/`positionY` 值强制为 50（cover 默认居中）

### SourcesTab 中涉及的位置

| 场景 | 是否禁用轴 |
|------|-----------|
| 顶部"当前背景"滑块 | ✅ 禁用无效轴 |
| 文件列表项的 override 标记 | 仅显示 `(x:55%, y:40%)`，无禁用概念 |

---

 const APP_CONFIG_DEFAULTS: AppConfig = {
     activate: true,
     opacity: 0.5,
     blur: 5,
-    positionX: 50,
-    positionY: 50,
     // ...rest unchanged
 }

`load()` 中追加迁移逻辑：
```ts
// 向前兼容：旧全局 positionX/Y 迁移到当前文件的 imageOverrides
const oldX = (stored as any)?.positionX
const oldY = (stored as any)?.positionY
if (oldX !== undefined || oldY !== undefined) {
    const cf = this.cfg.currentFile
    if (cf && !this.cfg.imageOverrides[cf]) {
        this.cfg.imageOverrides[cf] = {
            positionX: oldX ?? 50,
            positionY: oldY ?? 50,
        }
    }
    delete (this.cfg as any).positionX
    delete (this.cfg as any).positionY
    this.dirty = true
}
```

+ const override = imageOverrides[currentFile]
+ applyOverrides(override?.positionX, override?.positionY, 50, 50)

需 `import { applyOverrides }` 加入（当前 index.ts 未导入）。

#### 5a. 顶部新增"当前背景"区块

```svelte
<!-- 当前背景 -->
<div class="b3-label">
    <div class="fn__flex" style="align-items: center; gap: 12px;">
        <div class="fn__flex-1">
            <span class="ft__on-surface" style="font-size: 0.85em;">{i18n.currentFile}</span>
            <code class="fn__code" style="display: block; margin-top: 4px;">{formatCurrentFile(currentBg)}</code>
        </div>
        <div class="fn__flex-center" style="gap: 8px;">
            <div>
                <label style="font-size: 0.8em;">X</label>
                <input class="b3-slider fn__size50" type="range"
                    min="0" max="100" step="5"
                    bind:value={posX}
                    disabled={xDisabled}
                    title={xDisabled ? i18n.axisDisabledX : ''}
                    oninput={onPositionInput}
                    onchange={onPositionChange}
                />
            </div>
            <div>
                <label style="font-size: 0.8em;">Y</label>
                <input class="b3-slider fn__size50" type="range"
                    min="0" max="100" step="5"
                    bind:value={posY}
                    disabled={yDisabled}
                    title={yDisabled ? i18n.axisDisabledY : ''}
                    oninput={onPositionInput}
                    onchange={onPositionChange}
                />
            </div>
            {#if hasOverride}
                <button class="b3-button b3-button--text" onclick={resetPosition}
                    style="font-size: 0.8em;">{i18n.resetPosition}</button>
            {/if}
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
<div class="fn__hr"></div>
```

#### 5b. 新增状态和逻辑

```ts
let currentBg = $state<string | null>(null)
let posX = $state(50)
let posY = $state(50)
let hasOverride = $state(false)
let xDisabled = $state(false)
let yDisabled = $state(false)
let imgDims = $state<{ w: number; h: number } | null>(null)

function syncCurrentBg() {
    currentBg = configStore.get("currentFile")
    const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[currentBg ?? '']
    posX = override?.positionX ?? 50
    posY = override?.positionY ?? 50
    hasOverride = !!override
    detectImgDims()
}

function detectImgDims() {
    imgDims = null; xDisabled = false; yDisabled = false
    if (!currentBg || isVideoUrl(currentBg) || isDynamicUrl(currentBg)) return
    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => {
        imgDims = { w: img.naturalWidth, h: img.naturalHeight }
        updateDisabledAxes()
    }
    img.src = currentBg
}

function updateDisabledAxes() {
    if (!imgDims) return
    const vpW = document.documentElement.clientWidth
    const vpH = document.documentElement.clientHeight
    const imgAR = imgDims.w / imgDims.h
    const vpAR = vpW / vpH
    xDisabled = imgAR < vpAR - 0.01
    yDisabled = imgAR > vpAR + 0.01
}

function onPositionInput() {
    // 实时预览
    changePosition(posX, posY)
}

function onPositionChange() {
    const overrides = { ...configStore.get("imageOverrides") }
    if (posX === 50 && posY === 50) {
        delete overrides[currentBg!] // 恢复默认则删除
    } else {
        overrides[currentBg!] = { positionX: posX, positionY: posY }
    }
    configStore.set("imageOverrides", overrides)
    configStore.save()
    hasOverride = !!overrides[currentBg!]
}
```

需要在 `onMount` 中调用 `syncCurrentBg()`。

#### 5c. 文件列表项追加 override 标记

在文件项 `{file.name}` 后追加：

```svelte
{#if configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]}
    <span style="color: var(--b3-theme-on-surface); font-size: 0.8em; margin-left: 6px;">
        (x:{configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url].positionX}%,
         y:{configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url].positionY}%)
    </span>
{/if}
```

```ts
import { changePosition, applyOverrides } from "../../services/bgRender"
import { classifyFileType, isDynamicUrl } from "../../constants"
```

### 7. I18n 新增 key

| key | zh_CN | en_US |
|-----|-------|-------|
| `resetPosition` | `重置为默认` | `Reset to Default` |
| `axisDisabledX` | `图片高度已填满，左右位置无法调整` | `Image height fills viewport, horizontal position cannot be adjusted` |
| `axisDisabledY` | `图片宽度已填满，上下位置无法调整` | `Image width fills viewport, vertical position cannot be adjusted` |

---

### 不改动的文件

- `src/services/bgRender.ts` — `applyOverrides()` 已存在，`changePosition()` 不变
- `src/services/sourceManager.ts` — 无关
- `src/ui/dialogs/` — 无关
- `src/ui/settings/ThemeTab|AdvancedTab|AboutTab.svelte` — 无关
- `src/libs/` — 无关
- `src/utils/` — 无关

---

### 边界情况

| 场景 | 处理 |
|------|------|
| 无当前背景 (`currentFile`=null) | 隐藏整个"当前背景"区块 |
| 当前背景是视频 | X/Y 滑块可用，不检测分辨率 |
| 当前背景是动态 URL | X/Y 滑块可用，不检测分辨率 |
| 用户设回 50/50 | 删除 `imageOverrides` 中该条目 |
| 被禁用的轴 | 滑块 disabled + title tooltip，值强制 50 |
| 窗口 resize 后 AR 变化 | 需监听 `resize`（或在 `oninput` 时重新计算） |
| 旧配置有 positionX/Y | 迁移到 `imageOverrides[currentFile]` |

---

### 风险

1. **`delete (cfg as any).positionX`** — TS 类型不安全但运行时安全，仅在迁移阶段执行一次
2. **resize 监听** — 若频繁 resize 需防抖。建议仅监听 `onMount`/`currentFile` 变化时计算，resize 不触发重算（用户 resize 后重新打开设置面板自然刷新）
3. **`new Image()` 跨域** — `file://` 协议无跨域限制；`assets/` 和 `public/` 路径同源，可正常读取 `naturalWidth`

---

```svelte
{#each group.files as file}
    {@const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]}
    <label class="b3-list-item b3-list-item--narrow b3-list-item--hide-action"
        class:b3-list-item--focus={selectedItem?.url === file.url}
        onclick={() => setAsBackground(file)}

                aria-label={i18n.delete}
                onclick={(e) => { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); deleteFile(file) }}
                ...
            >
                <svg><use xlink:href="#iconTrashcan"></use></svg>
            </span>
        {/if}
        {#if override}
            <span class="b3-list-item__action b3-tooltips b3-tooltips__w"
                aria-label={i18n.resetPosition}
                onclick={(e) => { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); clearOverride(file.url) }}
                ...
            >
                <svg><use xlink:href="#iconFullscreenExit"></use></svg>
            </span>
        {/if}
    </label>
{/each}
```

`clearOverride()` 函数：

```ts
function clearOverride(url: string) {
    const overrides = { ...configStore.get("imageOverrides") }
    delete overrides[url]
    configStore.set("imageOverrides", overrides)
    configStore.save()
    // 如果清的是当前背景，更新滑块
    if (url === currentBg) {
        posX = 50; posY = 50
        hasOverride = false
        changePosition(50, 50)
    }
}
```

#### 5d. `savePositionOverride` 函数

```ts
function savePositionOverride() {
    const overrides = { ...configStore.get("imageOverrides") }
    if (posX === 50 && posY === 50) {
        delete overrides[currentBg!]
    } else {
        overrides[currentBg!] = { positionX: posX, positionY: posY }
    }
    configStore.set("imageOverrides", overrides)
    configStore.save()
    hasOverride = !!overrides[currentBg!]
}
```

#### 5e. 新增状态变量

```ts
let currentBg = $state<string | null>(null)   // currentFile 的镜像
let posX = $state(50)
let posY = $state(50)
let hasOverride = $state(false)
let xDisabled = $state(false)
let yDisabled = $state(false)
```

`syncCurrentBg()` 在 `onMount` 中调用，且需监听 `currentFile` 变化：

```ts
function syncCurrentBg() {
    currentBg = configStore.get("currentFile")
    const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[currentBg ?? '']
    posX = override?.positionX ?? 50
    posY = override?.positionY ?? 50
    hasOverride = !!override
    detectRelevantAxis()
}
```

#### 5f. Phase 5: 分辨率检测

```ts
function detectRelevantAxis() {
    xDisabled = false; yDisabled = false
    if (!currentBg) return
    // 视频和动态URL不检测
    const ext = currentBg.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? ''
    if (VIDEO_EXTS.has('.' + ext)) return
    if (isDynamicUrl(currentBg)) return

    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => {
        const imgAR = img.naturalWidth / img.naturalHeight
        const vpW = document.documentElement.clientWidth
        const vpH = document.documentElement.clientHeight
        if (vpW === 0 || vpH === 0) return
        const vpAR = vpW / vpH
        xDisabled = imgAR < vpAR - 0.01
        yDisabled = imgAR > vpAR + 0.01
        // 若被禁轴，强制该轴值为 50
        if (xDisabled) posX = 50
        if (yDisabled) posY = 50
    }
    img.src = currentBg
}
```

需从 `constants` 导入 `VIDEO_EXTS` 和 `isDynamicUrl`。

---

### I18n

| key | zh_CN | en_US |
|-----|-------|-------|
| `axisDisabledX` | `图像已填满屏幕高度，左右移动无效` | `Image fills viewport height, horizontal shift has no effect` |
| `axisDisabledY` | `图像已填满屏幕宽度，上下移动无效` | `Image fills viewport width, vertical shift has no effect` |
| `resetPosition` | `重置位置` | `Reset Position` |

---

### 保持不变

- `resetPosition` 按钮只出现在**文件列表项的右侧**（`#iconFullscreenExit`），不出现在顶部当前背景行
- 顶级当前背景行：滑块拖回 50/50 即删除 override

---

要开始实现吗？

  "newString": "    let dynamicUrls = $state<string[]>([])\n    let customDynamicUrls = $state<string[]>([])\n\n    let currentBg = $state<string | null>(null)\n    let posX = $state(50)\n    let posY = $state(50)\n    let hasOverride = $state(false)\n    let xDisabled = $state(false)\n    let yDisabled = $state(false)\n\n    function detectRelevantAxis() {\n        xDisabled = false; yDisabled = false\n        if (!currentBg) return\n        const ext = '.' + (currentBg.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')\n        if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return\n        if (isDynamicUrl(currentBg)) return\n\n        const img = new Image()\n        img.onload = () => {\n            const imgAR = img.naturalWidth / img.naturalHeight\n            const vpW = document.documentElement.clientWidth\n            const vpH = document.documentElement.clientHeight\n            if (vpW === 0 || vpH === 0) return\n            const vpAR = vpW / vpH\n            xDisabled = imgAR < vpAR - 0.01\n            yDisabled = imgAR > vpAR + 0.01\n            if (xDisabled) posX = 50\n            if (yDisabled) posY = 50\n        }\n        img.src = currentBg\n    }\n\n    function syncCurrentBg() {\n        currentBg = configStore.get(\"currentFile\")\n        const override = configStore.get(\"imageOverrides\")[currentBg ?? '']\n        posX = override?.positionX ?? 50\n        posY = override?.positionY ?? 50\n        hasOverride = !!override\n        detectRelevantAxis()\n    }\n\n    function savePositionOverride() {\n        if (!currentBg) return\n        const overrides = { ...configStore.get(\"imageOverrides\") }\n        if (posX === 50 && posY === 50) {\n            delete overrides[currentBg]\n        } else {\n            overrides[currentBg] = { positionX: posX, positionY: posY }\n        }\n        configStore.set(\"imageOverrides\", overrides)\n        configStore.save()\n        hasOverride = !!overrides[currentBg]\n    }\n\n    function clearOverride(url: string) {\n        const overrides = { ...configStore.get(\"imageOverrides\") }\n        delete overrides[url]\n        configStore.set(\"imageOverrides\", overrides)\n        configStore.save()\n        if (url === currentBg) {\n            posX = 50; posY = 50\n            hasOverride = false\n            changePosition(50, 50)\n        }\n    }",

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 18:46:51*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

Let me analyze the three bugs:

1. **Video preview doesn't stop when hovering over image**: When using `onmouseover` to trigger `selectPreview`, the video `src` is not cleared when switching to an image preview. The video element still has `src` set, so it keeps playing. Need to clear `previewVideoSrc` when selecting an image preview.

2. **Recenter button should be before delete button**: In the file list items, the order should be: recenter (iconFullscreenExit) first, then delete (iconTrashcan) last. Currently it seems delete is first.

3. **File list override marker doesn't update immediately after adjusting X/Y in top section**: The `{@const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]}` is computed once during render. But adjusting the X/Y sliders only calls `savePositionOverride()` which updates configStore and saves. Since the `groups` array isn't invalidated, the Svelte template doesn't re-render the file list items. Need to trigger a re-render or use a different approach.

Let me read the current state of the file to see what changes the user made.

</details>

234:         groups = groups
235:     }
236: 
237:     function openAssetDirDialog() {
238:         showAssetsDirDialog((paths: string[]) => {
239:             for (const dir of paths) addAssetFolder(dir)
240:         })
241:     }
242: 
243:     function openLocalDirDialog() {
244:         showLocalDirDialog((path: string) => {
245:             addLocalFolder(path)
246:         })
247:     }
248: 
249:     function addAssetFolder(dir: string) {
250:         if (!dir) return
251:         devLog("[bgCover] addAssetFolder:", dir)
252:         const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs"), dir]
253:         configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
254:         configStore.save()
255:         refreshAll()
256:     }
257: 
258:     function addLocalFolder(path: string) {
259:         if (!path) return
260:         devLog("[bgCover] addLocalFolder:", path)
261:         const folders = [...configStore.get("localFolders"), path]
262:         configStore.set("localFolders", folders)
263:         configStore.save()
264:         refreshAll()
265:     }
266: 
267:     function removeGroup(i: number) {
268:         const g = groups[i]
269:         devLog("[bgCover] removeGroup:", g.type, g.configKey)
270:         const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
271:         const wasCurrentInGroup = g.files.some(f => f.url === currentFile)
272:         if (g.type === 'assets') {
273:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("assetDirs")]
274:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
275:             if (idx >= 0) {
276:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
277:                 configStore.set("assetDirs", dirs)
278:                 configStore.save()
279:             }
280:         } else if (g.type === 'local') {
281:             const dirs = [...configStore.get("localFolders")]
282:             const idx = dirs.indexOf(g.configKey)
283:             if (idx >= 0) {
284:                 dirs.splice(idx, 1)
285:                 configStore.set("localFolders", dirs)
286:                 configStore.save()
287:             }
288:         }
289:         clearPreview()
290:         if (wasCurrentInGroup) {
291:             reselectBackground()
292:         }
293:         refreshAll()
294:     }
295: 
296:     function setAsBackground(item: ImageItem) {
297:         devLog("[bgCover] setAsBackground:", item.name)
298:         configStore.set("currentFile", item.url)
299:         configStore.save()
300:         if (item.type === 'image') {
301:             renderImage(item.url)
302:         } else {
303:             renderVideo(item.url)
304:         }
305:         syncCurrentBg()
306:         const ov = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[item.url]
307:         if (ov) changePosition(ov.positionX ?? 50, ov.positionY ?? 50)
308:     }
309: 
310:     function selectPreview(item: ImageItem) {
311:         if (selectedItem?.url === item.url) {
312:             clearPreview()
313:             return
314:         }
315:         selectedItem = item
316:         if (item.type === 'image') {
317:             loadPreview(item.url)
318:         } else {
319:             previewVideoSrc = item.url
320:         }
321:     }
322: 
323:     function clearPreview() {
324:         if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
325:         selectedItem = null
326:         previewSrc = null
327:         previewObjectUrl = null
328:         previewVideoSrc = null
329:     }
330: 
331:     function loadPreview(url: string) {
332:         if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
333:         previewObjectUrl = null
334:         previewSrc = null
335:         fetch(url)
336:             .then(r => r.blob())
337:             .then(b => {
338:                 if (selectedItem?.url === url) {
339:                     previewObjectUrl = URL.createObjectURL(b)
340:                     previewSrc = previewObjectUrl
341:                 }
342:             })
343:             .catch(() => {})
344:     }
345: 
346:     async function clearCache() {
347:         const group = groups.find(g => g.type === 'upload')
348:         if (!group || group.files.length === 0) return
349:         const imgCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'image').length
350:         const vidCount = group.files.filter(f => f.type === 'video').length
351:         const parts: string[] = []
352:         if (imgCount > 0) parts.push(`${imgCount} ${i18n.imageCount}`)
353:         if (vidCount > 0) parts.push(`${vidCount} ${i18n.videoCount}`)
354:         const confirmed = await new Promise<boolean>(resolve => {
355:             confirmDialog({
356:                 title: i18n.clearCacheTitle,
357:                 content: `${i18n.clearCacheConfirm} ${parts.join('、')}`,                confirm: () => resolve(true),
358:                 cancel: () => resolve(false),
359:                 width: "360px",
360:             })
361:         })
362:         if (!confirmed) return
363:         devLog("[bgCover] clearCache:", group.files.length, "files")
364:         const wasCurrentDeleted = group.files.some(f => f.url === configStore.get("currentFile"))
365:         for (const file of group.files) {
366:             await removeFile(file.apiPath)
367:         }
368:         if (wasCurrentDeleted) await reselectBackground()
369:         refreshAll()
370:     }
371: 
372:     function openInFileManager(group: SourceGroup) {
373:         const wsDir = (window as any).siyuan?.config?.system?.workspaceDir ?? ''
374:         let absPath = group.path
375:         if (group.type === 'upload' || group.type === 'assets') {
376:             absPath = wsDir + absPath
377:         }
378:         try {
379:             const shell = (window as any).require?.('electron')?.shell
380:             if (shell) {
381:                 shell.openPath(absPath)
382:             } else {
383:                 const { exec } = (window as any).require?.('child_process') ?? {}
384:                 if (exec) {
385:                     const cmd = process.platform === 'darwin' ? 'open' : process.platform === 'win32' ? 'explorer' : 'xdg-open'
386:                     exec(`${cmd} "${absPath}"`)
387:                 }
388:             }
389:         } catch { /* ignore */ }
390:     }
391: 
392:     async function reselectBackground() {
393:         configStore.set("currentFile", null)
394:         await configStore.save()
395:         await (window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.randomSelect?.()
396:         if (!configStore.get("currentFile")) {
397:             configStore.set("currentFile", pickDefaultBackground())
398:             await configStore.save()
399:             ;(window as any).bgCoverPlugin?.plugin?.applyBackground?.()
400:         }
401:     }
402: 
403:     async function deleteFile(file: ImageItem) {
404:         devLog("[bgCover] deleteFile:", file.name)
405:         const wasCurrent = file.url === configStore.get("currentFile")
406:         await removeFile(file.apiPath)
407:         if (wasCurrent) await reselectBackground()
408:         refreshAll()
409:     }
410: 
411:     function pickMultipleFiles() {
412:         setupMultipleFilePicker(() => { refreshAll() })
413:     }
414: 
415:     function pickFolderFiles() {
416:         setupFolderFilePicker(() => { refreshAll() })
417:     }

433:         })
434:     }
