### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 18:46:51*

*[step-start part]*

💭 **Reasoning:**

<details>
<summary>Click to expand reasoning</summary>

I can see the three bugs clearly now:

**Bug 1: Video preview doesn't stop when switching to image**

In `selectPreview()` (line 310-321):
```ts
function selectPreview(item: ImageItem) {
    if (selectedItem?.url === item.url) {
        clearPreview()
        return
    }
    selectedItem = item
    if (item.type === 'image') {
        loadPreview(item.url)
    } else {
        previewVideoSrc = item.url
    }
}
```

When switching from video to image, the `loadPreview()` function does:
```ts
function loadPreview(url: string) {
    if (previewObjectUrl) URL.revokeObjectURL(previewObjectUrl)
    previewObjectUrl = null
    previewSrc = null
    fetch(url)... // async
}
```

It nulls `previewSrc` but does NOT null `previewVideoSrc`. Since the template renders:
- If `previewVideoSrc` → show video
- Else if `previewSrc` → show image

`previewVideoSrc` is still set from the previous hover, so the video keeps playing while the new image loads async.

Fix: In `selectPreview`, before setting `previewVideoSrc`, we should also clear `previewVideoSrc`. And in `loadPreview`, clear `previewVideoSrc` too.

Actually, the simplest fix is: always clear `previewVideoSrc` when switching to image type:
```ts
if (item.type === 'image') {
    previewVideoSrc = null
    loadPreview(item.url)
}
```

**Bug 2: Reorder buttons - recenter before delete**

Currently:
```
<span delete> </span>  (686-695)
{#if override}
    <span recenter> </span>  (696-705)
{/if}
```

The delete button always comes first, then the recenter button. The user wants recenter first, delete last:
```
{#if override}
    <span recenter> </span>
{/if}
<span delete> </span>
```

**Bug 3: File list override marker doesn't update after XY adjustment**

The override marker uses `{@const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]}` which is a reactive `@const`. In Svelte 5, `@const` creates a constant in the template that is recomputed when the surrounding data changes.

Looking at the template:
```svelte
{#each group.files as file}
    {@const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]}
```

Since `configStore.get("imageOverrides")` returns a new object each time (snapshot), and the `@const` depends on `configStore.get()` which is NOT reactive... Actually, in Svelte 5, `@const` is like a derived, but it depends on which variables change. Since `groups` (the each loop) doesn't change when we save overrides, the `@const` is not re-evaluated.

The fix is to make the override markers reactive. One approach:
- Track a `positionVersion` counter that increments on save/clear
- Use that counter to force re-evaluation

Or simpler: in `savePositionOverride()` and `clearOverride()`, trigger `groups = groups` to force Svelte to re-render.

Actually, the `groups = groups` reassignment does trigger reactivity in Svelte 5 with `$state`. Let me try that.

Let me apply all three fixes.

</details>

看清楚了，三个 bug 都很明确。开始修复：

### Bug 4: Disabled slider visual

The user wants disabled sliders to be visually distinct. The fix is simple CSS:

```svelte
<input class="b3-slider fn__size50" type="range"
    disabled={xDisabled}
    style:opacity={xDisabled ? "0.4" : "1"}
    ...
/>
```

`groups = groups` 在 Svelte 5 中没有触发 `{#each}` 重渲染——数组引用相同，`@const` 读的是非响应式的 `configStore.get()`，所以标记不会更新。

## 计划

### 3. 真正修复响应式更新

**根因**：`@const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]` 中的 `configStore.get()` 不是 Svelte 响应式源。`groups = groups` 不触发 `{#each}` 重新求值 `@const`。

**方案**：改用 `groups = groups.slice()`（新数组引用强制 `{#each}` 重渲染），并在 `savePositionOverride()` 和 `clearOverride()` 中同时调用。

`SourcesTab.svelte` 改动：

```diff
- groups = groups
+ groups = groups.slice()
```

两处：`savePositionOverride()` 末尾和 `clearOverride()` 末尾。

### 4. disabled 滑块视觉区分

**方案**：disabled 时加 `style:opacity` 混入 `0.4` 透明度。

```diff
  <input class="b3-slider fn__size50" type="range"
      min="0" max="100" step="5"
      bind:value={posX}
      disabled={xDisabled}
+     style:opacity={xDisabled ? "0.4" : ""}
      title={xDisabled ? i18n.axisDisabledX : ''}
      oninput={() => changePosition(posX, posY)}
      onchange={savePositionOverride}
  />
```

X 和 Y 两个滑块都加。

共改动 `SourcesTab.svelte` 2 个函数 + 2 个 input 元素。要开始吗？

In Svelte 5, `{#each}` without an explicit key uses identity as the key. So `group` identity determines whether the DOM is preserved. When we do `groups.slice()`, the `group` objects are the same, so Svelte preserves the DOM and skips re-rendering the children.


This creates entirely new references for both groups and files arrays, forcing Svelte to re-render the entire `{#each}` tree.

</details>

## 根因定位

问题不在 `groups.slice()` —— 它确实触发了 `{#each groups}` 的重渲染，但 Svelte 5 的 `{#each}` 用 `===` 按 item 身份做 key diff。`slice()` 后的 `groups[0]` 仍然是同一个对象引用，Svelte 判断该项"未变"，**跳过该项子模板的重渲染**，所以 `@const override` 不会被重新求值。

```
groups = groups.slice()
         ↓
groups[0] === 原 groups[0]  →  跳过该项 DOM 更新
         ↓
{#each group.files as file}  →  group.files 也是同一引用，同样跳过
         ↓
@const override = configStore.get(...)  →  未重新求值，标记不变
```

## 方案

将 `groups.slice()` 改为深克隆一层，让所有 `group` 和 `files` 引用都变成新的：

```
savePositionOverride() / clearOverride() 末尾：
  groups = groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))
```

这样 Svelte 的 `{#each}` diff 认为**所有 item 都是新的**，强制重新渲染，`@const` 被重新求值。

> 代价：`toggleGroup` 展开/折叠状态会丢失。需额外处理。

## 确认

展开/折叠状态需要保留吗？也就是调整完 XY 后，之前展开的 group 应该保持展开？如果需要，我改用 `$derived.by` + version 计数器方案，不依赖深克隆。

*[step-finish part]*

### 🤖 Assistant
*2026-05-19 18:46:51*

同时还发现，修改后调用 window.siyuan.storage["siyuan-plugin-background-cover"] ， 重置后里面的overrides的值也没有发生变化，是同一个原因引起来的吗

```ts
let renderVersion = $state(0)

// In savePositionOverride and clearOverride:

{#each group.files as file, j (file.url + renderVersion)}
```

```svelte
{#each group.files as file (file.url + ':' + overridesVersion)}
```

This forces Svelte to treat all items as new when `overridesVersion` changes, causing full re-render including `@const` re-evaluation. The key changes, so items are fully unmounted and remounted.

Actually wait, changing the key to force re-mount is even more expensive. 

The simplest correct fix: deep clone the groups array but preserve collapse state.

```ts
groups = groups.map(g => ({
    ...g,
    files: [...g.files],
}))
```

This creates new references for all groups AND all files arrays, triggering `{#each groups}` to re-render items, which then re-renders `{#each group.files}`, and `@const override` is re-evaluated.

The collapse state is preserved because we spread `g` which includes `collapsed`.

## 根因分析：两个独立问题

### 问题 3（UI 标记不更新）

`groups = groups.slice()` 只换了最外层数组引用。`{#each groups as group}` diff 时发现 `group === 原group`，跳过该项。内层 `{#each group.files as file}` 同理。

`@const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]` 依赖 `file` 身份变化才重新求值，而 `file` 始终是同一对象引用，所以**永远不更新**。

### 问题 4（storage 不更新）

`savePositionOverride()` 和 `clearOverride()` 中 `configStore.save()` 是 async 但**没有 `await`**。`save()` 内部 `setLocalStorageVal` 是 fetch API 调用，未 await 时异步 flew away。用户紧接着查 `window.siyuan.storage` 时 fetch 还没完成。

两个问题**不相关**：一个是 Svelte 身份 diff，一个是异步等待。

---

## 方案

### Fix 1: UI 标记更新

`savePositionOverride()` / `clearOverride()` 末尾用浅克隆替换 `groups.slice()`：

```ts
groups = groups.map(g => ({
    ...g,
    files: [...g.files],
}))
```

- 每个 `group` 对象和新 `files` 数组都是新引用
- `collapsed` 等字段通过 spread 保留，展开状态不丢失
- `{#each}` 检测到 item 身份变化 → 全量重渲染 → `@const override` 重新求值

### Fix 2: storage 持久化

将 `savePositionOverride()` 和 `clearOverride()` 改为 `async`，`await configStore.save()`。

---

The user is asking me to trace the data flow of `imageOverrides` to understand where the "disconnect" is. They want me to analyze the current synchronization flow and identify the breakpoints before I propose any fixes. Since I'm in plan/read-only mode, I should just analyze and explain.

Let me trace the flow:

**Flow 1: User adjusts X/Y slider in SourcesTab (top section)**
1. User drags slider → `oninput` fires → `changePosition(posX, posY)` → canvas/video updates immediately ✅
2. User releases slider → `onchange` fires → `savePositionOverride()`
3. `savePositionOverride()`:
   - Reads `configStore.get("imageOverrides")` → gets current overrides object
   - Creates new `overrides` object with changes
   - `configStore.set("imageOverrides", overrides)` → sets `this.cfg.imageOverrides = overrides`, `dirty = true` ✅
   - `configStore.save()` → calls `setLocalStorageVal(STORAGE_KEY, this.cfg)` async, **NOT awaited** ❌
   - `hasOverride = !!overrides[currentBg]` ✅
   - `groups = groups.slice()` → tries to trigger re-render ❌ (doesn't work, as we established)

**Flow 2: User clicks recenter button in file list**
1. `clearOverride(file.url)` fires
2. Creates new overrides without the entry
3. `configStore.set("imageOverrides", overrides)` ✅
4. `configStore.save()` → **NOT awaited** ❌
5. `posX/posY` reset if current bg, `changePosition(50, 50)` ✅
6. `groups = groups.slice()` ❌

**Flow 3: Reading overrides back**
- `configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]` reads from `this.cfg.imageOverrides` which is in-memory. This works correctly because `set()` already mutated `this.cfg`.

**Breakpoints identified:**

**Breakpoint A: `configStore.save()` not awaited**
- `save()` is async, calls `setLocalStorageVal()` which is a fetch API call
- Not awaited → caller returns before fetch completes → `window.siyuan.storage` not updated yet
- Also: `save()` has `dirty` guard. If called without await and then called again before first save completes, the second call might see `dirty=false` from the first call's `setLocalStorageVal` callback... wait no, `dirty` is set to `false` AFTER `await setLocalStorageVal`. If we don't await the first save, the second call starts while first is still pending - but the first hasn't reset dirty yet because it hasn't completed. So dirty would still be true. But we set dirty=true again anyway in the second `set()` call. 

Actually, the real issue with not awaiting: the promise might reject silently, and the error is swallowed. Also, concurrent saves without await could interleave in unexpected ways.

**Breakpoint B: Svelte reactivity**
- `groups = groups.slice()` doesn't change item identity for `{#each}`
- `@const override = configStore.get(...)` is not re-evaluated

**The synchronization flow the user expects:**
```
Slider change → savePositionOverride()
    ├─ configStore.set() → this.cfg updated in memory ✅
    ├─ configStore.save() → storage persisted      ❌ (not awaited)
    ├─ hasOverride flag → top section reactive      ✅
    └─ groups update → file list re-renders         ❌ (slice() doesn't work)
```

The user's intuition is right: there should be ONE trigger that pushes both UI and storage updates. Currently the flow is broken at two points.

A clean approach would be: make `savePositionOverride` async, await the save, then force re-render. Something like:

```ts
async function savePositionOverride() {
    // ... update configStore ...
    await configStore.save()  // persist
    // Force reactive update
    groups = groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))
}
```

But wait - `onchange` handler calling an async function... The Svelte `onchange` for range inputs should be fine with async.

Let me present this analysis clearly.

</details>

## 当前数据同步流程追踪

```
滑块 onchange → savePositionOverride()
                      │
         ┌────────────┼────────────┐
         ▼            ▼            ▼
  configStore.set()  save()      groups.slice()
  this.cfg更新 ✅    未await ❌   未触发重渲染 ❌
         │            │            │
         ▼            ▼            ▼
   内存生效        storage未写    file列表不更新
```

### 两个断点

| 断点 | 位置 | 原因 |
|------|------|------|
| **A** | `configStore.save()` 未 `await` | 异步 fetch 飞出，调用者不等结果。紧接着读 `window.siyuan.storage` → 旧值 |
| **B** | `groups = groups.slice()` | 新数组但内部 `group` / `files` 引用不变，`{#each}` 身份 diff 判定未变 → 跳过 `@const` 求值 |

### 你的直觉是对的

两条分支本该是**同一根触发链**：`set("imageOverrides", ...)` 更新内存后，应该**同时**推进 `save()` 和 UI。当前是两条分支各自断联：

```
理想：set() ─┬─ await save()  → storage ✅
            └─ 触发 UI 重渲染 → file 列表标记更新 ✅

现状：set() ─┬─ save() 飞出   → storage ❌
            └─ groups.slice() → 不触发重渲染 ❌
```

### 修复思路

两处用相同模式：`await` 持久化完成后，浅克隆 groups 触发全量重渲染。

```ts
// savePositionOverride: onchange 改 async
async function savePositionOverride() {
    // ... set ...
    await configStore.save()
    groups = groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))
}

// clearOverride 同款
async function clearOverride(url: string) {
    // ... delete ...
    await configStore.save()
    // ... reset posX/posY if currentBg ...
    groups = groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))
}
```

> `groups.map` 浅克隆保留 `collapsed` 字段，展开状态不丢失。

groups.map 浅克隆保留 collapsed 字段，展开状态不丢失。这个需要

The safest fix for the `finally` scope issue is to move the `currentFile` declaration outside the `try` block:

```ts
private applyBackground() {
    devLog("[bgCover] applyBackground: start")
    const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")  // move outside try
    try {
        // ...rest uses currentFile from outer scope...
    } finally {
        // ...uses currentFile from outer scope...
    }
}
```

This eliminates any potential scope issue with `try/finally`.

For the UI issue (#3 still not updating), let me think...

The user says they see `[bgCover] config save` in logs, which means `save()` IS being called. But the file list marker doesn't update until collapsing/expanding.

Wait, if `[bgCover] config save` appears, then `savePositionOverride()` is reaching `await configStore.save()`. After that, `groups = groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))` should execute. This creates a completely new array of new objects.

But `groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))` only shallow-clones top-level properties of `g`. The `collapsed` property would be preserved via spread.

Hmm, wait. Let me think about this more carefully. When we do:
```ts
groups = groups.map(g => ({
    ...g,
    files: [...g.files],
}))
```

Each `g` is a `SourceGroup` object:
```ts
interface SourceGroup {
    type: 'upload' | 'assets' | 'local'
    label: string
    path: string
    removable: boolean
    files: ImageItem[]
    inaccessible: boolean
    collapsed: boolean
    configKey: string
}
```

Spreading `g` copies all properties, and then `files: [...g.files]` creates a new array. So both the group object AND the files array are new references.

But wait - `{ ...g }` creates a NEW plain object. The original `g` is a reactive `$state` proxy object in Svelte 5. When we spread it and create a plain object, we lose the reactive proxy. Then when we assign `groups = groups.map(...)`, Svelte creates NEW proxies for the new array and its items.

So the flow should be:
1. `groups` is a `$state` reactive proxy
2. `groups = groups.map(...)` assigns a new plain array
3. Svelte detects the assignment and creates new reactive proxies for the new array and its items
4. The template re-renders because the state changed
5. `{#each groups as group}` sees all new group references
6. `{#each group.files as file}` sees all new file references
7. `@const override = configStore.get(...)` is re-evaluated for each file

This SHOULD work. Unless there's something else going on...

Could the issue be that `groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))` somehow doesn't trigger the Svelte 5 reactivity properly? Let me think...

In Svelte 5, `$state` proxies detect assignments. When you do `groups = newValue`, Svelte detects the assignment and proxies `newValue`. But `newValue` is a fresh array of plain objects. Svelte should re-render the template for any state change.

Wait - could the issue be that the collapse state is LOST? When we spread `g` and create a plain object, and Svelte proxies it, could the `collapsed` field somehow be different? Let me trace:

1. Original: `groups[0].collapsed = false` (part of reactive proxy)
2. After map: `groups[0].collapsed = false` (copied from spread, but now in a plain object)
3. After assignment: Svelte creates new proxy with `collapsed = false`

This should preserve the collapsed state correctly.

Hmm, but maybe the issue is that Svelte 5 treats `groups = groups.map(...)` as equivalent to `groups = groups` (no change)? In Svelte 5, `$state` uses `Object.is()` for comparison? No, for arrays, Svelte should detect the reference change.

Actually, I just realized something. The user said the collapse state is preserved when they manually collapse/expand. That means the `collapsed` field IS being preserved. But the marker text isn't updating. So the issue is specifically about `@const override` not re-evaluating.

Let me think about `@const` in Svelte 5. `@const` creates a local constant in the template. It's derived from the surrounding reactive context. The `@const` is re-evaluated when:
1. The block it's in is re-created (e.g., new item in `{#each}`)
2. Or when one of its dependencies changes

Since `configStore.get("imageOverrides")` is a function call, Svelte can't track it as a reactive dependency. So `@const` is only re-evaluated when the `{#each}` item identity changes.

If `groups.map()` successfully creates new references, then `{#each}` should re-create items... but maybe Svelte 5 uses keys to match items?

Looking at the template:
```svelte
{#each group.files as file}
```

There's no key expression. In Svelte 5, `{#each}` without a key uses identity-based diffing with `===`. If the new files array has the same objects in the same order, Svelte might match them by index and not re-create items.

Wait, no. `groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))` creates a NEW files array with the SAME file objects. So `files[0]` in the new array is still `===` to the old `files[0]`. Svelte matches them and doesn't re-render.

THAT'S THE PROBLEM! `[...g.files]` creates a new array but the items (file objects) are the same references. So `{#each group.files as file}` diffing sees `file === oldFile` and doesn't re-evaluate `@const`.

The fix: we need to also create new file object references. Either:
- Deep clone files too
- Or use a different approach like a version counter

Deep cloning files is expensive but correct:
```ts
groups = groups.map(g => ({
    ...g,
    files: g.files.map(f => ({ ...f })),
}))
```

This creates new file objects too. Then `{#each group.files as file}` sees new references and re-evaluates `@const`.

But this is wasteful for large lists. A version counter approach would be cleaner:

```ts
let overridesVersion = $state(0)

// In savePositionOverride and clearOverride:
overridesVersion++

// In template, use version in @const:
{@const _v = overridesVersion}
{@const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]}
```

Wait, but `@const _v = overridesVersion` creates a dependency on `overridesVersion` change, which then forces re-evaluation of the next `@const`. In Svelte 5, `@const` variables are serial (each depends on the previous), so changing `_v` would force the next `@const` to re-evaluate... but that only works if `@const override` depends on `_v`.

Actually, I'm not sure this works. Let me think of a cleaner approach.

Option: Use a `$derived` lookup map instead of `@const`.

```ts
let overridesVersion = $state(0)
let overrideMap = $derived.by(() => {
    void overridesVersion  // dependency
    return configStore.get("imageOverrides")
})
```

Then in the template:
```svelte
{@const override = overrideMap[file.url]}
```

This should work because `overrideMap` is a `$derived` that changes when `overridesVersion` changes. But `@const override` depends on `overrideMap` which is reactive... hmm, `@const` can't track `$derived` changes unless it's used in a reactive context.

Actually, in Svelte 5 templates, `@const` IS in reactive context. If `overrideMap` is a reactive state, then `@const override = overrideMap[file.url]` should re-evaluate when `overrideMap` changes.

Wait, but the `{#each}` skip prevents `@const` from being re-evaluated at all. Even if `overrideMap` changes, if the `{#each}` item isn't re-created, `@const` isn't re-evaluated.

So the real fix is to ensure `{#each}` re-creates items. And the simplest way to do that without deep cloning is to use a key that includes the version:

```svelte
{#each group.files as file (file.url + ':' + overridesVersion)}
```

This changes the key when `overridesVersion` changes, forcing Svelte to treat all items as new, re-creating them (and thus re-evaluating `@const`).

This is the right approach. Let me also think about edge cases:
- Performance: For small lists (most users have <100 images), this is fine.
- Collapse state: Group collapse is at a higher level, not affected by file-level key changes.
- Preview state: Selected item and preview might reset - need to check.

Actually, using `(file.url + ':' + overridesVersion)` as key means Svelte will unmount and remount each file item, which resets any local state. The only local state in file items is... none. The preview state (`selectedItem`) is at the component level, not in the file item.

But the `mouseover` handlers and focus states might be reset. That's acceptable.

Let me finalize the plan.

</details>

## 根因分析

### Error: `currentFile is not defined`

看第 199 行，`currentFile` 在 `try` 块内 `const` 声明，ES 标准下 `finally` 可以访问，但某些构建环境（esbuild/Vite 优化）可能对 `try/finally` 变量提升处理有差异。

**最稳妥修复**：把 `const currentFile` 提到 `try` 前面，保证所有路径可见：

```diff
     private applyBackground() {
         devLog("[bgCover] applyBackground: start")
+        const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
         try {
-            const currentFile = configStore.get("currentFile")
             devDebug(...)
```

### UI 标记仍不更新

之前的 `groups.map(g => ({ ...g, files: [...g.files] }))` 确实创建了新 group 和新数组，但 `files` 数组内**每一项 file 仍是原对象引用**。`{#each group.files as file}` diff 时 `file === oldFile` → 跳过该 item → `@const override` 永不重新求值。

```
旧: files[0] === 新: files[0]  →  Svelte 判定未变 → 跳过 @const
需: files[0] !== 新: files[0]  →  Svelte 判定为新 → 重新求值 @const
```

---

## 方案

**换用 key 方案**，不深克隆 data，只引入 `overridesVersion` 计数器：

```svelte
<script>
let overridesVersion = $state(0)
</script>

<!-- 每个 file item 用 key=(url + version) -->
{#each group.files as file (file.url + ':' + overridesVersion)}
    {@const override = configStore.get("imageOverrides")[file.url]}
    <!-- ... -->
{/each}
```

`solvePositionOverride` / `clearOverride` 末尾只做 `overridesVersion++`，不再碰 `groups`。

对比：

| 方案 | 改动量 | 数据拷贝 | collapse 保留 | 
|------|--------|----------|---------------|
| 深克隆 files 内 item | 2 行 | O(n) 内存分配 | ✅（但浪费） |
| key + version 计数器 | 3 行 | 0 | ✅ |

---

The user is asking about why the X/Y axis disabling doesn't work for video backgrounds. Let me look at the `detectRelevantAxis()` function in SourcesTab.svelte to understand the current logic.

Looking at the code I already read:

```ts
function detectRelevantAxis() {
    xDisabled = false; yDisabled = false
    if (!currentBg) return
    const ext = '.' + (currentBg.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
    if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return  // ← 视频直接跳过
    if (isDynamicUrl(currentBg)) return

    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => {
        const imgAR = img.naturalWidth / img.naturalHeight
        // ...
    }
    img.src = currentBg
}
```

Yes, video detection is explicitly skipped at line 55 because `new Image()` can't handle video files - it would fail to load. But actually, `video` elements DO have `videoWidth` and `videoHeight` properties after metadata loads, which can give us the dimensions.

However, there's a more subtle issue: for video with `object-fit: cover`, the same aspect ratio logic applies. We could get the video dimensions by creating a hidden `<video>` element, loading the source, and reading `videoWidth`/`videoHeight` from the `loadedmetadata` event.

But this adds complexity (DOM element creation, cleanup). And the video might not be accessible from the current context (CORS, etc.).

A simpler alternative: for videos uploaded by the user, we already have the URL. We can create a `<video>` element (without adding to DOM), set `preload="metadata"`, and listen for `loadedmetadata`.

Let me think about the cleanest implementation:

```ts
function detectRelevantAxis() {
    xDisabled = false; yDisabled = false
    if (!currentBg) return
    if (isDynamicUrl(currentBg)) return

    const ext = '.' + (currentBg.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
    if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
        detectVideoDims(currentBg)
        return
    }

    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => {
        const imgAR = img.naturalWidth / img.naturalHeight
        const vpW = document.documentElement.clientWidth
        const vpH = document.documentElement.clientHeight
        if (vpW === 0 || vpH === 0) return
        const vpAR = vpW / vpH
        xDisabled = imgAR < vpAR - 0.01
        yDisabled = imgAR > vpAR + 0.01
        if (xDisabled) posX = 50
        if (yDisabled) posY = 50
    }
    img.src = currentBg
}

function detectVideoDims(url: string) {
    const video = document.createElement('video')
    video.preload = 'metadata'
    video.onloadedmetadata = () => {
        const imgAR = video.videoWidth / video.videoHeight
        const vpW = document.documentElement.clientWidth
        const vpH = document.documentElement.clientHeight
        if (vpW === 0 || vpH === 0) return
        const vpAR = vpW / vpH
        xDisabled = imgAR < vpAR - 0.01
        yDisabled = imgAR > vpAR + 0.01
        if (xDisabled) posX = 50
        if (yDisabled) posY = 50
        video.removeAttribute('src')
        video.load()
    }
    video.src = url
}
```

But there's a problem: `video.onloadedmetadata` fires asynchronously, and we need to set the `xDisabled`/`yDisabled` state variables AFTER the metadata loads. This is the same async pattern as the image `onload`. So the slot codes work the same way.

Wait, actually looking at the current `detectRelevantAxis()`, the image `onload` already sets `xDisabled`/`yDisabled` in a callback. So the same pattern works for video.

But there's a subtlety: for local files (file://) and assets, the video might not load properly in a hidden element without being added to the DOM? Actually, in most browsers, a video element doesn't need to be in the DOM to load metadata. Setting `src` and listening for `loadedmetadata` should work.

However, for `file://` protocol, there might be restrictions in Electron's webview. And for `assets/` paths, the video should load fine.

Let me also consider: should I refactor the common logic (calculating which axis is disabled based on dimensions) into a shared function?

Actually let me just present the plan concisely. The fix is straightforward - add video dimension detection using a `<video>` element's `loadedmetadata` event, analogous to how we use `Image.onload`.

The user is asking a specific question: "是因为无法获取视频的x和y分辨率吗？" - Yes, that's exactly why. The current code explicitly skips video files. I need to explain this and propose the fix.

But I'm in plan-only mode, so I can only analyze and plan.

</details>

是的，正是这个原因。`detectRelevantAxis()` 中视频路径直接 `return` 跳过，因为 `new Image()` 无法加载 `.mp4` 等视频格式：

```ts
// src/ui/settings/SourcesTab.svelte:55
if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) return  // ← 直接跳过，无尺寸检测
```

### 修复方案

视频可以用 `<video>` 元素的 `loadedmetadata` 事件获取 `videoWidth`/`videoHeight`，逻辑与图片完全对称：

```ts
function detectRelevantAxis() {
    xDisabled = false; yDisabled = false
    if (!currentBg) return
    if (isDynamicUrl(currentBg)) return

    const ext = '.' + (currentBg.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? '')
    if (VIDEO_EXTS.has(ext)) {
        detectVideoDims(currentBg)
        return
    }

    // 图片：现有逻辑不变
    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => updateDisabledAxes(img.naturalWidth, img.naturalHeight)
    img.src = currentBg
}

function detectVideoDims(url: string) {
    const video = document.createElement('video')
    video.preload = 'metadata'
    video.onloadedmetadata = () => {
        updateDisabledAxes(video.videoWidth, video.videoHeight)
        video.removeAttribute('src')
        video.load()  // 释放资源
    }
    video.src = url
}

function updateDisabledAxes(w: number, h: number) {
    const imgAR = w / h
    const vpW = document.documentElement.clientWidth
    const vpH = document.documentElement.clientHeight
    if (vpW === 0 || vpH === 0) return
    const vpAR = vpW / vpH
    xDisabled = imgAR < vpAR - 0.01
    yDisabled = imgAR > vpAR + 0.01
    if (xDisabled) posX = 50
    if (yDisabled) posY = 50
}
```

改动量：提取 `updateDisabledAxes` 公共函数（现有图片 `onload` 回调复用），新增 `detectVideoDims` 函数，`detectRelevantAxis` 中视频分支从 `return` 改为调用 `detectVideoDims`。

约 15 行改动，只改 `SourcesTab.svelte`。要执行吗？
